--- Commit Message ---
LU-13802 llite: add read & write switch thresholds

The main criteria for switching to from buffered IO to
hybrid is IO size.  This adds that switching.  The correct
size for cutover is not the same for read and write, so we
have separate checks for read and write.

These checks are elaborated on in further patches, adding
different thresholds based on the backing storage type.

Adding the switching thresholds is what really enables
hybrid IO, so we have to adjust a number of tests which
assume buffered IO.

There are a few obscure hang bugs which have been difficult
to track down, and we are past feature freeze, so this patch
now leaves hybrid IO disabled by default.

Signed-off-by: Patrick Farrell <patrick.farrell@oracle.com>

--- Message (Patrick Farrell, 2023-10-08 17:59:00.000000000) ---
Patch Set 1:

I am curious to get feedback on this.

My testing results showed that the cutover point is different for READ io than for WRITE IO.

For read, it is > 8 MiB, and for write, it is > 2 MiB.  This is a very significant difference.

So I've put them in as a separate thresholds.  This is instead of a single threshold like in Yingjin's patch.

Does this seem OK?  One threshold would be nice but it does not match my benchmarks, so I think we need two.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2024-02-12 05:50:43.000000000) ---
Patch Set 16:

It would make sense to push a separate patch to update i_size on the client after successful DIO write completion.  If the client gets the size from the OSTs on stat() then it will override this, but if the client doesn't stat the file on close then at least it will have something to send to the MDS. The LSOM code is forgiving of getting different sizes from clients.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2024-02-12 05:51:07.000000000) ---
